\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ -\/\ \ exponent\ -\/\ an\ integer\ value\ with\ a\ sign}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ mantissa\ must\ be\ pushed\ into\ the\ left\ side\ that\ is\ the\ highest\ bit\ from\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ mantissa\ must\ be\ one\ (of\ course\ if\ there's\ another\ value\ than\ zero)\ -\/-\/\ this\ job}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ (pushing\ bits\ into\ the\ left\ side)\ is\ doing\ by\ Standardizing()\ method}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ for\ example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ we\ want\ to\ store\ value\ one\ (1)\ into\ our\ Big\ object\ we\ must:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ -\/\ \ \ set\ mantissa\ to\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ -\/\ \ \ set\ exponent\ to\ 0}}
